							<h1 class="post-title"><a href="http://myscienceacademy.org/2013/01/03/27-science-fictions-that-became-science-facts-in-2012/">27 Science Fictions That Became Science Facts In 2012</a> 
				<!--					<sup class="post-comment"><a href="http://myscienceacademy.org/2013/01/03/27-science-fictions-that-became-science-facts-in-2012/#comments" title="Comment on 27 Science Fictions That Became Science Facts In 2012">392</a></sup>

				</h1>
			 
	
		    

		    

				       
			<div class="bottomcontainerBox" style="background-color:#FAFAFA;">

<article itemscope itemtype="http://nik.io/v1/schema/Article">
      <span itemprop="lastModifiedDate" content="2013-01-03 13:30:43"></span><span itemprop="title" content="27 Science Fictions That Became Science Facts In 2012"></span><span itemprop="categories" content="Articles~Feature~Physics~Technology"></span><span itemprop="tags" content="3D~Brain~DNA~earth~Google~implants~invisibility~Life~Mind~NASA~Planet~printer~robot~Solar System~space"></span><span itemprop="srcType" content="wordpress.org"></span><span itemprop="permalink" content="http://myscienceacademy.org/2013/01/03/27-science-fictions-that-became-science-facts-in-2012/"></span><span id= "wpLogin" itemprop="wpLogin" content=""></span>We may never have our flying cars, but the future is here. From creating fully functioning artificial leaves to hacking the human brain, science made a lot of breakthroughs this year.</p>
<h2>1. Quadriplegic Uses Her Mind to Control Her Robotic Arm</h2>
<p><img class="aligncenter size-medium wp-image-5356" title="enhanced-buzz-27396-1355847916-5" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-27396-1355847916-5-590x332.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="332" /><br />
At the University of Pittsburgh, the neurobiology department worked with 52-year-old Jan Scheuermann over the course of 13 weeks to create a robotic arm controlled only by the power of Scheuermann&#8217;s mind.<br />
The team implanted her with two 96-channel intracortical microelectrodes. Placed in the motor cortex, which controls all limb movement, the integration process was faster than anyone expected. On the second day, Jan could use her new arm with a 3-D workspace. By the end of the 13 weeks, she was capable of performing complex tasks with seven-dimensional movement, just like a biological arm.<br />
To date, there have been no negative side effects.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: gizmodo.com</span></em></p>
<h2>2. DARPA Robot Can Traverse an Obstacle Course</h2>
<p><iframe src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/FFGfq0pRczY" frameborder="0" width="590" height="332"></iframe><br />
Once the robot figures out how to do that without all the wires, humanity is doomed.<br />
DARPA was also hard at work this year making robots to track humans and run as fast as a cheetah, which seems like a great combination with no possibility of horrible side effects.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: jwherrman</em></span></p>
<h2>3. Genetically Modified Silk Is Stronger Than Steel</h2>
<p><img class="size-medium wp-image-5357" title="enhanced-buzz-29236-1355865550-1" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-29236-1355865550-1-590x442.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="442" /><br />
<span style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic;">Photo Courtesy of Indigo Moon Yarns.</span></p>
<p>At the University of Wyoming, scientists modified a group of silkworms to produce silk that is, weight for weight, stronger than steel. Different groups hope to benefit from the super-strength silk, including stronger sutures for the medical community, a biodegradable alternative to plastics, and even lightweight armor for military purposes.<br />
<span style="color: #888888;"><em>Source: bbc.co.uk</em></span></p>
<h2>4. DNA Was Photographed for the First Time</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5377" title="enhanced-buzz-29231-1355865033-5" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-29231-1355865033-5-590x444.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="444" /><br />
Using an electron microscope, Enzo di Fabrizio and his team at the Italian Institute of Technology in Genoa snapped the first photos of the famous double helix.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: newscientist.com / via: davi296</span></em></p>
<h2>5. Invisibility Cloak Technology Took a Huge Leap Forward</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5378" title="enhanced-buzz-28471-1355862628-4" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-28471-1355862628-4-590x590.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="590" /><br />
British Columbia company HyperStealth Biotechnology showed a functioning prototype of its new fabric to the U.S. and Canadian military this year. The material, called Quantum Stealth, bends light waves around the wearer without the use of batteries, mirrors, or cameras. It blocks the subject from being seen by visual means but also keeps them hidden from thermal scans and infrared.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: toxel.com</em></span></p>
<h2>6. Spray-On Skin</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5380" title="enhanced-buzz-19212-1355862934-1" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-19212-1355862934-1-590x358.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="358" /><br />
ReCell by Avita Medical is a medical breakthrough for severe-burn victims. The technology uses a postage stamp–size piece of skin from the patient, leaving the donor site with what looks like a rug burn. Then the sample is mixed with an enzyme harvested from pigs and sprayed back onto the burn site. Each tiny graft expands, covering a space up to the size of a book page within a week. Since the donor skin comes from the patient, the risk of rejection is minimal.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: news.discovery.com</em></span></p>
<h2>7. James Cameron Reached the Deepest Known Point in the Ocean</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5381" title="enhanced-buzz-12372-1355869429-3" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-12372-1355869429-3-590x602.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="602" /><br />
Cameron was the first solo human to reach the bottom of the Mariana Trench. At 6.8 miles deep, it is perhaps more a more alien place to scientists than some foreign planets are. The 2.5-story &#8220;vertical torpedo&#8221; sub descended over a period of two and a half hours before taking a variety of samples.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: news.nationalgeographic.com</em></span></p>
<h2>8. Stem Cells Could Extend Human Life by Over 100 Years</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5382" title="enhanced-buzz-29090-1355865809-13" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-29090-1355865809-13-590x442.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="442" /><br />
When fast-aging elderly mice with a usual lifespan of 21 days were injected with stem cells from younger mice at the Institute for Regenerative Medicine in Pittsburgh, the results were staggering. Given the injection approximately four days before they were expected to die, not only did the elderly mice live — they lived threefold their normal lifespan, sticking around for 71 days. In human terms, that would be the equivalent of an 80-year-old living to be 200.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: news.nationalgeographic.com</em></span></p>
<h2>9. 3-D Printer Creates Full-Size Houses in One Session</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5383" title="enhanced-buzz-9372-1355866863-6" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-9372-1355866863-6-590x331.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="331" /><br />
The D-Shape printer, created by Enrico Dini, is capable of printing a two-story building, complete with rooms, stairs, pipes, and partitions. Using nothing but sand and an inorganic binding compound, the resulting material has the same durability as reinforced concrete with the look of marble. The building process takes approximately a fourth of the time as traditional buildings, as long as it sticks to rounded structures, and can be built without specialist knowledge or skill sets.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: gizmag.com</span></em></p>
<h2>10. Self-Driving Cars Are Legal in Nevada, Florida, and California</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5384" title="enhanced-buzz-9855-1355867279-0" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-9855-1355867279-0-590x384.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="384" /><br />
Google started testing its driverless cars in the beginning of 2012, and by May, Nevada was the first state to take the leap in letting them roam free on the roads. With these cars logging over 300,000 autonomous hours so far, the only two accidents involving them happened when they were being manually piloted.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: en.wikipedia.org</span></em></p>
<div style="display: block; margin: 0px auto 20px !important; width: 100%; text-align: center;"><script type="text/javascript">// <![CDATA[
google_ad_client = "ca-pub-6965588547261395"; /* Text link */ google_ad_slot = "7732882042"; google_ad_width = 468; google_ad_height = 15;
// ]]&gt;</script><br />
<script type="text/javascript" src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js">// <![CDATA[</p>
<p>// ]]&gt;</script></div>
<h2>11. Voyager I Leaves the Solar System</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5385" title="enhanced-buzz-8630-1355930344-6" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-8630-1355930344-6-590x344.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="344" /><br />
Launched in 1977, Voyager I is the first manmade object to fly beyond the confines of our solar system and out into the blackness of deep space. It was originally designed to send home images of Saturn and Jupiter, but NASA scientists soon realized eventually the probe would float out into the great unknown. To that end, a recording was placed on Voyager I with sounds ranging from music to whale calls, and greetings in 55 languages.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: space.com</em></span></p>
<h2>12. Custom Jaw Transplant Created With 3-D Printer</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5386" title="enhanced-buzz-9874-1355867609-7" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-9874-1355867609-7-590x369.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="369" /><br />
A custom working jawbone was created for an 83-year-old patient using titanium powder and bioceramic coating. The first of its kind, the successful surgery opens the door for individualized bone replacement and, perhaps one day, the ability to print out new muscles and organs.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: telegraph.co.uk</span></em></p>
<h2>13. Rogue Planet Floating Through Space</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5387" title="enhanced-buzz-15730-1355930351-2" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-15730-1355930351-2-590x377.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="377" /><br />
Until this year, scientists knew planets orbited a star. Then, in came CFBDSIR2149. With four to seven times the mass of Jupiter, it is the first free-floating object to be officially defined as an exoplanet and not a brown dwarf.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: sciencenews.org</em></span></p>
<h2>14. Chimera Monkeys Created from Multiple Embryos</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5388" title="enhanced-buzz-430-1355868123-0" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-430-1355868123-0-590x332.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="332" /><br />
While all the donor cells were from rhesus monkeys, the researchers combined up to six distinct embryos into three baby monkeys. According to Dr. Mitalipov, &#8220;The cells never fuse, but they stay together and work together to form tissues and organs.&#8221; Chimera species are used in order to understand the role specific genes play in embryonic development and may lead to a better understanding of genetic mutation in humans.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: bbc.co.uk</em></span></p>
<h2>15. Artificial Leaves Generate Electricity</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5389" title="enhanced-buzz-12396-1355869429-3" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-12396-1355869429-3-590x389.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="389" /><br />
Using relatively inexpensive materials, Daniel G. Nocera created the world&#8217;s first practical artificial leaf. The self-contained units mimic the process of photosynthesis, but the end result is hydrogen instead of oxygen. The hydrogen can then be captured into fuel cells and used for electricity, even in the most remote locations on Earth.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: sciencedaily.com</span></em></p>
<h2>16. Google Goggles Bring the Internet Everywhere</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5390" title="enhanced-buzz-12399-1355869428-7" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-12399-1355869428-7-590x332.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="332" /><br />
Almost everyone has seen the video of Google&#8217;s vision of the future. With their Goggles, everyday life is overlaid with a HUD (Head&#8217;s Up Display). Controlled by a combination of voice control and where the user is looking, the Goggles show pertinent information, surf the web, or call a loved one.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: heraldsun.com.au</span></em></p>
<h2>17. The Higgs-Boson Particle Was Discovered</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5393" title="enhanced-buzz-12319-1355869430-8" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-12319-1355869430-8-590x354.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="354" /><br />
Over the summer, multinational research center CERN confirmed it had discovered a particle that behaved enough like a Higgs boson to be given the title. For scientists, this meant there could be a Higgs field, similar to an electromagnetic field. In turn, this could lead to the scientists&#8217; ability to interact with mass the same way we currently do with magnetic fields.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: forbes.com</em></span></p>
<h2>18. Flexible, Inexpensive Solar Panels Challenge Fossil Fuel</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5394" title="enhanced-buzz-4208-1355869423-1" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-4208-1355869423-1-590x885.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="885" /><br />
At half the price of today&#8217;s cheapest solar cells, Twin Creeks&#8217; Hyperion uses an ion canon to bombard wafer-thin panels. The result is a commercially viable, mass-produced solar panel that costs around 40 cents per watt.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: extremetech.com</span></em></p>
<h2>19. Diamond Planet Discovered</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5395" title="enhanced-buzz-15055-1355930343-2" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-15055-1355930343-2-590x332.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="332" /><br />
An exoplanet made entirely of diamonds was discovered this year by an international research team. Approximately five times the size of Earth, the small planet had mass similar to that of Jupiter. Scientists believe the short distance from its star coupled with the exoplanet&#8217;s mass means the planet, remnants of another star, is mostly crystalline carbon.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: io9.com</span></em></p>
<h2>20. Eye Implants Give Sight to the Blind</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5396" title="enhanced-buzz-12371-1355869431-5" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-12371-1355869431-5-590x368.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="368" /><br />
Two blind men in the U.K. were fitted with eye implants during an eight-hour surgery with promising results. After years of blindness, both had regained &#8220;useful&#8221; vision within weeks, picking up the outlines of objects and dreaming in color. Doctors expect continued improvement as their brains rewire themselves for sight.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: telegraph.co.uk</span></em></p>
<div style="display: block; margin: 0px auto 20px !important; width: 100%; text-align: center;"><script type="text/javascript">// <![CDATA[
google_ad_client = "ca-pub-6965588547261395"; /* Text link */ google_ad_slot = "7732882042"; google_ad_width = 468; google_ad_height = 15;
// ]]&gt;</script><br />
<script type="text/javascript" src="http://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/show_ads.js">// <![CDATA[</p>
<p>// ]]&gt;</script></div>
<h2>21. Wales Barcodes DNA of Every Flowering Plant Species in the Country</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5397" title="enhanced-buzz-15773-1355872597-7" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-15773-1355872597-7-590x440.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="440" /><br />
<span style="font-size: 10px; font-style: italic;">Photo Courtesy of Virtual Tourist.</span></p>
<p>Led by the National Botanic Garden&#8217;s head of research and conversation, a database of DNA for all 1,143 native species of Wales has been created. With the use of over 5,700 barcodes, plants can now be identified by photos of their seeds, roots, wood, or pollen. The goal is to help researchers track things such as bee migration patterns or how a plant species encroaches on a new area. The hope is to eventually barcode both animal and plant species across the world.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: walesonline.co.uk</em></span></p>
<h2>22. First Unmanned Commercial Space Flight Docks with the ISS</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5398" title="enhanced-buzz-20766-1355873346-0" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-20766-1355873346-0-590x442.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="442" /><br />
SpaceX docked its unmanned cargo craft, the Dragon, with the International Space Station. It marked the first time in history a private company had sent a craft to the station. The robotic arm of the ISS grabbed the capsule in the first of what will be many resupply trips.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: nytimes.com</span></em></p>
<h2>23. Ultra-Flexible &#8220;Willow&#8221; Glass Will Allow for Curved Electronic Devices</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5400" title="enhanced-buzz-16277-1355873326-4" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-16277-1355873326-4-590x590.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="590" /><br />
Created by New York–based developer Corning, the flexible glass prototype was shown off at an industry trade show in Boston. At only 0.05mm thick, it&#8217;s as thin as a sheet of paper. Perhaps Sony&#8217;s wearable PC concept will actually be possible before 2020.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: bbc.co.uk</em></span></p>
<h2>24. NASA Begins Using Robotic Exoskeletons</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5401" title="enhanced-buzz-15077-1355930344-0" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-15077-1355930344-0-590x442.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="442" /><br />
The X1 Robotic Exoskeleton weighs in at 57 lbs. and contains four motorized joints along with six passive ones. With two settings, it can either hinder movement, such as when helping astronauts exercise in space, or aid movement, assisting paraplegics with walking.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: news.cnet.com</em></span></p>
<h2>25. Human Brain Is Hacked</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5402" title="enhanced-buzz-15028-1355930344-3" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-15028-1355930344-3-590x578.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="578" /><br />
Usenix Security had a team of researchers use off-the-shelf technology to show how vulnerable the human brain really is. With an EEG (electroencephalograph) headset attached to the scalp and software to figure out what the neurons firing are trying to do, it watches for spikes in brain activity when the user recognizes something like one&#8217;s ATM PIN number or a child&#8217;s face.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: extremetech.com</span></em></p>
<h2>26. First Planet with FOUR Suns Discovered</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5403" title="enhanced-buzz-31996-1355930303-1" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-31996-1355930303-1-590x332.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="332" /><br />
Discovered by amateur astronomers, the planet closely orbits a pair of stars, which in turn orbit another set of more distant stars. It&#8217;s approximately the size of Neptune, so scientists are still trying to work out how the planet has avoided being pulled apart by the gravitational force of that many stars.<br />
<span style="color: #999999;"><em>Source: io9.com</em></span></p>
<h2>27. Microsoft Patented the &#8220;Holodeck&#8221;</h2>
<p><img class="alignnone size-medium wp-image-5404" title="enhanced-buzz-18203-1355932329-0" src="http://d12tusb9bq3y6m.cloudfront.net/wp-content/uploads/2013/01/enhanced-buzz-18203-1355932329-0-590x345.jpg" alt="" width="590" height="345" /><br />
The patent suggests Microsoft wants to take gaming beyond a single screen and turn it into an immersive experience — beaming images all over the room, accounting for things like furniture, and bending the graphics around them to create a seamless environment.<br />
<em><span style="color: #999999;">Source: bbc.co.uk</span></em></p>
<p><span style="color: #999999;"><em>Found on:</em> <a href="http://buzzfeed.com" target="_blank"><span style="color: #999999;">buzzfeed.com</span></a></span></p>
<h1>And what do you think? Which one is the most important?</h1>

				<p>Beaming images all over the room and compensating for furniture sounds a lot like the multi-projector systems that already exist. For example, about nine years ago, I was talking with a researcher at UdeM (Montréal, QC) who was telling me the differences between the two systems developed in the same department. Both systems involved cloaking objects in the room using a camera that watches where projected pixels end up on the walls. One of them was used repeatedly at the SAT arts centre. I wonder what is actually covered by that patent, because this whole thing I just wrote about is well-documented prior art.</p>

			<div class="commententry">
							
				<p>Well, the problem would be that it would cost a lot in time and effort to get to the planet.  Then, to pay off that debt you would only have diamonds as &quot;currency.&quot;  Flooding the market with diamonds would reduce the value, making them no more valuable than much more common quartz, for example.  There might be a pay off in utility of the diamond for industrial uses, though.  And then, there is the use of the compact carbon as fuel.  An interesting thought, nonetheless.</p>
